Stagnation in Intestine Exports 162

Pig intestines were originally a type of export trade. In previous years, the export volume was quite considerable in the trade books. However, this year's business has plummeted, greatly affected by the global economic downturn. Germany, the United States, and other countries have stopped importing, resulting in business stagnation. In addition, no one consults about fresh intestines in this port. Therefore, the industry colleagues held an emergency meeting at the association's office on Sanma Road yesterday and resolved to submit a request to the Social Bureau to be forwarded to the Ministry of Industry for relief.

Inspection Report of Zhejiang Industrial Bank 163

The 46th inspection report of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank's issuance reserve states that the issuance of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank has always been completely separated from the business side, and the reserves are fully sufficient. On the 13th of this month, the accountant Yan Ouke inspected the cash reserve, which was more than 60%, and the guarantee reserve was less than 40%. Reading Q&A

Another Example of Studying International Issues (4) 168

However, we can also say with certainty here that this compromise is indeed extremely harsh on the Chinese nation. It clearly pushes the Chinese nation into the possibility of becoming a colony, which is a point that every researcher should be very wary of.

The above is naturally just a summary of the research on this topic. Please carry out a more detailed review yourself! This is a very interesting issue. We would also like to ask Mr. Zhao to compare the key points and research methods we have put forward with the opinions and views of the "international affairs commentator" that Mr. Zhao referred to. Where are the differences between us?

From this, we can see that theoretical learning is indeed not easy, and theoretical application is even more difficult. From this, we realize that purely abstract theoretical research can only make us scholars in the study, which is not very useful for the "people of the world." On the contrary, we can only truly grasp the theory from all practices, which has truly become an undeniable truth. But the former is easier to engage in, while the latter requires a lot of hard work. For example, in recent years, quite a few books on historical materialism have been introduced to China, but there are very few who can use it to apply to China's actual situation. What China needs now has gone beyond the boundaries of purely studying principles. Especially for people like us who live this kind of life, even if we want to read a few books on the original theory, it must be to apply it, so here, the editor has to specially propose that readers pay more attention to application, learn must apply, and don't just hold on to dead books.

Mr. Zhao's letter naturally also gave ordinary readers an opportunity to learn how to observe international issues. However, Mr. Zhao's letter also proves that the few articles we wrote before have not been fully understood by readers, or at least cannot be used to apply. We again propose to the readers, if you feel that some books on principles are difficult to read, it is best to pay more attention to the illustrated examples of using correct methods, that is, articles on research in various aspects. The things in the "Reading Q&A" column, of course, there are some that are worth reading by you.

In addition, we also hope that readers can put forward some of their own experiments in using methods to us (we should not be afraid of mistakes, afraid of being naive). Let us further promote the combination of reading true theory and practice in our lives.

Open-Air Court Installation Completed 178

After the Chinese Basketball Hall was burned down, a temporary open-air court was set up in front of the special grandstand of the baseball field for this preliminary selection. Vargas, Vice President of the Philippine Sports Association, issued a statement saying that the Philippines will act in accordance with the articles of association of the Games and does not want any country to violate the constitution of the Games.

Vice President of the Philippine Sports Association Announces Attitude (Jiji News Agency, Manila, 3rd) Vargas, Vice President of the Philippine Sports Association, issued a statement late on the 12th, explaining the attitude of the Philippine representatives at the round table conference in Shanghai. At the same time, he hoped that Japan would participate in this year's Games. The content roughly stated that if Japan had any new proposals, we would naturally consider them. We sincerely hope that Japan will come to the Philippines to participate in the Games. Speaker of the Upper House, Kane, is currently on his way back to the Philippines from the United States. Because Kane also serves as the President of the Sports Association, I will telegraph Kane to clarify the Philippine position to the Japanese Sports Association when he arrives. The Japanese Sports Association's inquiry telegram has been received. This association will hold a meeting of the Executive Committee of the Sports Association at 9:00 a.m. on the 14th to discuss countermeasures and decide on a reply. Before Dr. Tan went to Shanghai to attend the round table conference, this association instructed him to vote in favor of the puppet state's participation, but refused to adopt a majority vote system. A unanimous decision is required because we do not want any country to trample on the constitution of the Far Eastern Games.

The Philippine Sports Association Will Still Take the Established Policy (Jiji News Agency, Manila, 13th) The issue of the puppet state participating in the Far East Games caused a sudden dispute due to the breakdown of the round table conference in Shanghai. Vargas, Vice President of the Philippine Sports Association, will convene a standing committee meeting on the 14th to decide on the final attitude towards this issue. According to general observations, the Philippine Sports Association will follow the established policy and decide to unanimously decide on the puppet state's participation.

Japanese Sports Association Telegraphed Philippine Sports Association Again (Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 13th) Yesterday afternoon, the Japanese Sports Association received a telegram from Yamamoto, the representative in Shanghai, requesting that the content of the inquiry sent by the Japanese Sports Association to the Philippine Sports Association the day before be revised. It also received a telegram from Yamamoto to the Philippine Sports Association, requesting that the inquiry letter issued by the Japanese Sports Association be temporarily reserved. The executives of the Sports Association immediately held an executive meeting at the Central Pavilion yesterday afternoon. As a result of the discussion, it was clear that the Philippine side was distrustful, so an inquiry should be sent. They also telegraphed Representative 本 to immediately lift the request for the Philippines to reserve the inquiry letter. At 7 p.m., they continued to hold an emergency board meeting at the Marunouchi Hotel. As a result of the discussion, it was decided to explain that the points pointed out by Representative Yamamoto were not the main points of the inquiry to the Philippines, and to telegraph the Philippines again, recognizing the ultimatum of the previous night as valid. The meeting adjourned at 0:40 a.m. The main points of the re-telegram to the Philippines are as follows: It is said that Representative Yamamoto telegraphed your association to cancel the telegram sent by the Japanese Sports Association the previous night. This was due to a failure to understand the main parts of the previous telegram. This association does not require the puppet state's membership, only hopes to invite it to participate. Although there is no such provision in the constitution of the Games, there is a precedent for India's participation. Those who wish to participate should be carefully considered and cannot be rejected outright. Regarding this point, it is hoped that your association will reflect.

Ilanan Advocates Rejecting Japan's Proposal (Jiji News Agency, Manila, 13th) The Japanese Sports Association telegraphed the Philippine Sports Council, accusing it of breaking its promise, and telegraphed again on the 12th, urging it to invite the puppet state to participate in this Far East Games. Today, Mr. Ilanan, who is in charge of the Philippine Sports Association, made a statement on the 13th regarding this so-called new proposal, as follows: The Japanese Sports Association's proposal cites the practices before the current implementation, saying that the participation of a country does not require a unanimous vote and that the puppet state should be invited and allowed to participate in advance, but the Philippines will never recognize it, no matter how much it is urged. I believe that the Philippine Sports Council will naturally reject this kind of request.

Yamamoto and Matsuzawa Returned to Japan from Shanghai Yesterday (Jiji News Agency, Tokyo, 13th) Representatives Yamamoto and Matsuzawa took the Nagasaki Maru from Shanghai on the 13th and returned to Japan. They are scheduled to arrive in Tokyo at 5 p.m. on the 15th.

Japan Postponed the Far East Preliminary Selection Today (Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 13th) The Far East Games Preparatory Committee has decided to postpone the All-Japan Preliminary Selection Conference scheduled to be held on the 14th until the Philippine Sports Association replies and the Japanese Sports Association decides on its attitude.

Far East Games Football South China Preliminary Selection First Game Hong Kong Beats Guangzhou One to Zero Hong Kong Good at Attacking Guangzhou Good at Defending Li Huitang Contributes to Hong Kong Team 186

(Hong Kong Correspondence) The South China team preliminary selection for the Far East Games football, which has been prepared by both the Guangdong and Hong Kong sides for more than a month, was held at the South China Athletic Association Stadium on Caroline Hill in Hong Kong at 4 p.m. on the 8th. The second preliminary selection competition will be held in Guangzhou on the 14th. After the two preliminary selections are completed, the Guangdong and Hong Kong Sports Associations will carefully select the team, and then a joint team from Guangdong and Hong Kong will compete against the Shanghai joint team. Then, the elite players will be selected from the two teams to form the Chinese football team to attend the Far East Games and compete with teams from the Philippines, Japan, the Netherlands, India, etc.

Guangdong Team Loses Key Players On the 8th, the Guangdong team was forced to replace four key players, Chen Zhenhe, Xu Yahui, Mai Zhaohan, and Li Guozhao, with Huang Ruikai, Liu Qingcai, Li Jin, and Xiao Dianlian. The strength was inevitably affected. Fortunately, there were three key players in the back, Li Tiansheng, Tan Jiangbai, and Huang Jiliang, to defend, so there was no need to worry about the rear. If these three key players had not been working for the Guangdong team, the Hong Kong team could have done whatever it wanted. The opposing players are as follows:

Li Jin Yang Shuiyi

Li Guowei Feng Qingyu

Hong Kong Nearly in Danger At the beginning of the war, the Guangzhou side took advantage of the wind, and Feng Jingxiang, Hua Beihua, and Yang Shuiyi were quite active for a while. Feng Jingxiang picked left and right, galloping horizontally and vertically, and charging repeatedly. The Hong Kong side was almost in danger. Later, the Hong Kong team's central defenders stepped up their operations, and the arrogance of the Guangdong team was slightly reduced. Gradually, the morale of the Hong Kong team was better than that of the Guangdong team. At that time, Cao Guicheng, the flying general on the right wing, ran forward with the help of Liang Zhaozhi, the red-faced public in the middle. Li Huitang and Zheng Jiliang also advanced forward. All the capable players of the Hong Kong team gathered in front of the Guangdong team's formation. If it were not for Huang Jiliang's courage and wisdom, the Guangdong team would have lost its territory long ago.

No Win or Loss in the First Half After twenty minutes, Guangzhou relied on the wind again and rushed in, with Ye Beihua on the left and Feng Jingxiang in the middle making close contact. Song Guolun was also active, and the morale was boosted. During the melee, the referee Ou Jiesheng suddenly blew his whistle, indicating that the Hong Kong team had committed a handball near the goal seventeen yards away. This ball was kicked by the Guangdong team. Liu Qingcai concentrated and thought of the arrow successfully, but he used too much force, and the ball flew into the air. In the first half, Yang Shuiyi was extremely dutiful, but Li Guowei watched closely at all times, preventing him from shielding, which is a pity. In the second half, He Jiaqiang of the Hong Kong team did not play, and was supplemented by the fresh force Qu Bingming. The combat power was not affected much, and with the advantage of the wind, the ball king and the flying general were more active and completely occupied the advantage. The central defender line of the Guangzhou team almost lost its ability to resist, and the rear defenders Li and Tan felt exhausted. When it was eighteen minutes, the ball king Li Huitang got the ball from Zheng Jiliang's plate and shot it hard. The ball entered from the right corner of the goal, because of his strength, Jiliang finally could not save it. The audience was celebrating for the Hong Kong team.

Hong Kong Team Wins After the victory, the Guangzhou team tried to counterattack again and again, but was repeatedly repelled by the central defender line and could not succeed. In any case, the referee Ou Jiesheng's war whistle rang long, and the twenty-two warriors also obeyed the order to rest. In terms of individual skills, Feng Jingxiang, Li Tiansheng, and Tan 澕柏 of Guangzhou were the most outstanding. Ye Beihua's skills remained the same after the illness, but his strength was slightly worse, and he did not seem as brave as before. Huang Jiliang's defense was beyond reproach. Except for Liu Qingqing, the central defender seemed to have nothing to take. Li Huitang, Zheng Jiliang, and Cao Guicheng of the Hong Kong team performed the best. The central defender line Liang Rongzhao and Li Guowei were also not inferior. He Zuoxian was too weak, and Liang Xuanzan, the defender, had the same disease. Liu Mao also performed well. The goalkeeper Huang Huangji belonged to the B team of the South China, but the battle was generally good that day. It is intended that Huang is also a trainable material.

Ideal Lineup for South China As for the ideal lineup for the match between South China and East China, as far as I can see, it should be as follows: Goalkeeper Bao Jiaping or Huang Jiliang, defenders Li Tiansheng and Liu Mao, central defenders Li Guowei, Liang Rongzhao, Xu Yahui or Chen Zhenhe, forwards Ye Beihua, Li Huitang learn Feng Jingxiang, Zheng Jiliang, Cao Guicheng. Four Knights Difficult to Attend As for the list of the South China team, it will be decided after the second game. After the competition is completed, the South China team can be selected to compete against East China. Regarding the issue that the four knights cannot attend, the reporter asked Feng Jingxiang specifically. According to him, the four of them work in the same place. If they all attend the fast transport, it may be difficult to achieve.

Zhejiang Education Director Chen Bulei Resigns Old Illness Occurs Frequently, Recently Getting Worse 190

Chen Bulei, Director of the Education Department, has always been weak and has suffered from neurasthenia for many years. Since his illness last year, his physical condition has not recovered. The old illness occurs from time to time, and he has felt increasingly overwhelmed since the beginning of spring. Feeling that his sick body cannot bear the heavy responsibility for a long time, he has already earnestly resigned from all his current positions to the Executive Yuan yesterday, and separately submitted them to the Ministry of Education and the Provincial Government for forwarding. The letter of resignation stated, "An old illness occurs frequently, and recently it has been getting worse. Even slightly complicated affairs make me exhausted. In public, I cannot work consistently; in private, I am physically and mentally exhausted. I earnestly request permission to resign in order to emphasize public affairs," and so on. Chen had repeatedly requested to resign last year due to illness, but was retained by the various parties in the Yuan, Ministry, and Provincial Government, and was unable to obtain permission. It is reported that this time the intention to resign is extremely firm. In addition to formally submitting the request, he also met with Chairman Lu in person to earnestly explain the reasons for his request to retire. He also sent a personal letter to Minister Wang of the Ministry of Education, detailing his physical weakness and the suffering that forced him to seek retirement, and earnestly requested him to convey his wishes to the Yuan to ensure that the Central Government understood and approved his request.

Chronicles

Watching the Waterfall at Five Vents (Part 1) 200

— Huo Xueming

Arrived in 　　 City last night, watching the sunset 　 disappear, but not die, then dragging 　　　, out of the South Gate, along the Huansha Creek, went to the ancient 　　 Village 　 and visited the small Xishi Temple. Right here, I painfully witnessed the tragedy of the middle-aged nun 　　　 the young girl with hair in the Buddhist hall, and could not muster the mood of a poet to see the brilliant sunset spring scenery on the Golden Rooster Mountain across the river. I had to pick up a few red leaves that were not completely withered, and returned to the hotel to write a letter to Manli in Shanghai, but there was a bit of loneliness in the mood. So I didn't even bother with supper, and just took out the quilt to sleep, keeping my eyes open until dawn. This day was clear and refreshing, making people happy.

At about seven o'clock in the morning, I took a rickshaw and left the verdant ancient city, immersed in the misty sky all the way, following the Youlong Mountains north. Thrushes were singing in the mountains, quiet and cold. By the time I reached Caota Town, the sun had turned silver-gray. The scenery was so good all the way to Qingkou. To get from Qingkou to Five Vents Temple, you have to cross eighteen water streams. If it is not a dry season, you must hire a cradle-like bamboo raft, sit inside, and have porters carry you across the stream. But when I went, it had been sunny for more than a month, so I went barefoot, wearing straw sandals, rolled up my trousers, and leisurely passed through the stream. Only three miles away, the Five Vents Chan Temple came into view.

The Five Vents Temple was originally named Yong'an Temple. Anyone who comes to see the waterfall must eat and stay here due to time constraints. We went in and made arrangements with the monk Yinhong. After eating a meat lunch, we went to find the waterfall. The monks here do not abstain from killing, nor do they recite scriptures. They wear their hair on the left side, just like ordinary people.

The so-called Five Vents is a waterfall originating from Zikai Village. It refers to the spring water that gushes out from the various rock crevices in five upper and lower, winding stages. Under the guidance of the monk Yinhong, we went out of the north gate of the temple, walked a hundred steps on the stone road, and climbed a few steps of the Niudun Mountain. It was all bamboo forest, with green leaves covering the sky, but a wisp of sunlight flowed out from the shade, shining on the mountain path, as if printing a few floating white flowers. At this time, in the midst of ten thousand bamboos, we heard a loud spring sound. The closer we got, the louder the sound became. We were all looking up at the mountain, searching for the thunderous sound, but Yinhong tilted his head, stopped his feet, stretched out a finger, and pointed to the left, saying:

"Isn't that the Fifth Vent?"

Everyone was immediately surprised and stood still. Looking intently, a silver-shining python was hanging down on the towering stone wall, so thick and angrily, flying down from the air, hitting the eaves, making a fierce roar.

"Wow! Great!" I shouted, walking down the stone beach to the left, planning to sit there and watch it to my heart's content.

"There are even greater ones. Follow me, friends!" The monk was also interesting. He quickly walked up to Xiangtie Ridge, not using a cane, but running fast. We had no choice but to follow. The bold sound of the waterfall still remained in our ears, and the snow-white color of the spring still flowed before our eyes. I really didn't know what the so-called greater one was like? A curious mood encouraged my legs, not asking for mercy at all, and not resting at all, and actually made it up half the mountain in one breath, and there was no road here. We entered the path between the bushes and went down through the thorns. The green grass that no one had stepped on was very slippery. The grass grew so high that it often swallowed the whole body. The small figures were faintly visible in the dense bushes, and the sound of "rustling" came out. Only heard a scream in front, and the man slipped and fell, and then someone fell again, and all the canes almost lost their effectiveness.

Watching the Waterfall at Five Vents (Part 2) 201

— Huo Xueming

With great difficulty, we climbed to the top of the mountain and looked down, seeing the hanging waterfall of the Second Vent, divided into two strands, hitting obliquely on the stone, rushing into the square pool. The locals call this pool the Coffin Pool. The water jumped out of the pool and flowed down the stone slope for twenty or thirty feet, just like the rushing of the Tianqiao Waterfall in Mount Lushan. From here, turning to the left and down, we saw a stone gap like a dragon's head, followed by a stone slab with holes, just like a wellhead, with two rows of waterfalls hanging in the mouth. The momentum was surging, spewing snow and splashing jade, and thousands of flowers of water rose and fell, like an old dragon coughing there. This is the First Vent. After watching for a long time, the sound of the spring was not very majestic, probably because it was too far away. Then we climbed down the dangerous cliff, using our hearts and minds in the vines, climbing down step by step, holding a cane in one hand and grabbing the wild grass with thorns in the other. Blood oozed out of the skin drop by drop, but I forgot the pain. I was paying attention to my greater life, hanging on a small tree on a hundred-foot cliff, on a clump of wild grass. I also trembled and looked down at the deep abyss. I was crawling on the upright stone wall. What if... ah! I dare not think, what if any one of my hands lost its grip? What if the small holly tree that my foot was stepping on was uprooted? What if the stone corner that my hand was holding loosened and rolled down! Wow! Today I know the true meaning of traveling in the mountains! Do people sitting in sedan chairs smoking cigars understand the dangerous peaks and bad valleys? No wonder Li Daoyuan of the Waterways Classic talked about "the middle three vents cannot be reached"! And now the literati who write travelogues about the Five Vents are still picking up Li Daoyuan's stale words and dare not experience the dangers themselves, which is really embarrassing!

As a result of our hands and feet working together, we finally reached the Third Vent. The Third Vent is a two-fold flying spring, flowing over the large stones covered with accumulated algae, horizontally and vertically five or six feet wide, all rushing straight down urgently, just like the flood that suddenly broke through Zhanggongchang in Hankou the year before last; this place is full of ocher red large stones, black large stones, and tea green large stones, all horizontally and obliquely up and down. Walking on them, you will meet straw shoes, and if you are not careful, you will slip and fall. Therefore, when climbing down, you have to lean your back against the stone and slowly slide down, and when getting up, you have to tightly cover your chest on the stone and try your best to lift your weight with both hands to succeed. As for the cane, because both it and the stone are hard things, they cannot bear the force, so you must not use it. The rushing flying spring washes these slippery stones day and night. It is poured into the stone crevices and flows to the empty valley. This is the Third Vent, which is the widest of the Five Vents.

Tiptoeing on the big stones, we arduously crossed the Third Vent. In front of the wind, there was a loud sound of the waterfall, but we couldn't see the shadow. This is the Fourth Vent. Seeing a black stone crouching on the side, like a majestic crouching tiger; we climbed up one after another. Climbing on the stone tip that was facing the ground and was full of water, we stretched out our heads and peered into the stone cave that looked like two doors. We only saw the side of a cluster of flying waterfalls, not knowing where it drifted out from, tending to the deep pool, rushing down in two folds, urgently and rapidly, and its momentum was irresistible. This is the most dangerous of the Five Vents. Standing there, the world was completely surrounded by the sound of the spring, and we were described as being particularly small and particularly weak.

It is a pity that such a mountain tour, even life is at risk of sacrifice at any time, it is inconvenient to carry a camera to take it into the lens, it is really a pity!

That night, I stayed in the wild temple of Donglongqiu and had a tired and terrifying spring dream.

Traveling Gear 202

— Shou Juan

Traveling and playing in the water is the only pleasure in life. If it can be relieved with traveling gear, then the pleasure will last longer. Westerners have a basket that combines knives, forks, cups, plates, water bottles, wine flagons, etc., for use when traveling for a picnic; there is also a kind of travel stool, made in a triangular shape and made of canvas, which can be folded up and used as a walking stick. The manufacturing is very precise, which is convenient for tourists. In recent years, travel groups in our country have sprung up like mushrooms. On good days in spring and autumn, boats and vehicles are endless, and all of them are tourists. However, when we search for it in domestic goods, we cannot get a single piece of traveling gear. Isn't this a pity? Reading the notes of Wu Danchan, a Qing dynasty person, he said that there was a Jiang Jusheng in Huangshan who called himself the Layman Woyun'an. He made traveling gear, hollowing out willow wood to make a flat stone (that is, a carrying pole, the stone sound is a pole), coated with lacquer, shiny, dark, and strong. He carried two bamboo baskets, with several layers of baskets, hanging the flat stone on both ends. What was stored inside were pocket-sized poems and rhymes, five-color Song Dynasty imitation note paper, fine inkstone, stone brush, ink, etc.; and copper tea and wine utensils, secret-color food utensils, sand pots, earthenware basins, cooking stoves, fan fire chopsticks, fire flint, lacquer rest pots, mottled bamboo chopsticks, etc., which were placed layer by layer, and outside was a wet dried gourd, palm cattail cushion hanging on the flat stone. Every time he traveled, everyone knew it was the Layman Woyun'an's items. I think these traveling gears are quite well-equipped, but it is necessary to carry them with a flat pole, acting like a porter, which seems too burdensome, and is not suitable for modern people. If we can take the best of it and modify it, then every tourist will definitely have one as a special item.

Miscellaneous Poems on the Lake 203

— Zhan Lu

The spring holiday of the twenty-third year of the Republic of China has been spent between the Six Bridges and the Three Temples! The spring scenery on the lake is certainly very good; but, I myself inexplicably feel that there is a kind of melancholy trace floating in my heart, alas! It cannot be blown away. It cannot be cut off. It is a cloud of sorrow! 　　 On the Shanghai-Hangzhou road, I only feel that outside the car window, more layers of curtains have been added; this is not an ordinary curtain, it is a product of the Great Nature Company, weaving the fine rain threads into sparse and dense curtains. I said sadly; "It's a bit too much to hurry to West Lake to listen to the rain." The Zhu brothers who were traveling with me, Xiaogu and Zao Wu, said in unison; "Maybe it's God adding makeup to Xizi." When we arrived in Hangzhou, it was already night. The next day, it was newly cleared, and when we looked up, we saw that the good mountains seemed to have been bathed. This night's rain was simply a makeup poem given by God. I made a quatrain;

The lake and mountains are newly cleared and their appearance has changed, the willows are green and the grass is fragrant; I recognized Xishi in the paintings, last night's rain was the makeup.

A mobile concert was opened on West Lake. Male and female students floating on the lake were playing music and singing in dragonfly-style boats; West Lake was originally charming and beautiful, but with this water music, it became even more charming and beautiful. However, in such a world, if there is a Huan Ziye who hears the song, he will just call Naibao! I made a quatrain;

A light boat chases the light waves, playing the flute and singing on the water; If there is a Huan Ziye from the past, he should also scratch his head and ask what to do.

I heard an unfortunate thing on the lake. The American Consul General, Mr. Keyinhan, brought his wife to visit the lake and mountains. His wife suddenly suffered an acute illness and died in a hospital in Hangzhou. People said it was meningitis. The Weaver Girl star sank, and of course there was sadness for the Silver River! I made a quatrain;

Bringing family to enjoy the spring, the joy was not yet in full bloom, suddenly the happy intestines turned into sad intestines! The Star Weaver Girl sank and mourned the Silver River, heaven and earth are both vast and vague.

The nickname of King Qian Wusu was Poliu. When he was born, the room was full of strange phenomena. His father wanted to abandon him, but an old woman helped him to raise him, so he was called Poliu. Later, he used three thousand iron crossbows to shoot back the tide. Although the matter is close to mythology, it makes people feel energetic when they hear it. Now the Yinghai storm is evil. Where will another Qian Poliu come to shoot back the tide? I made a quatrain;

Wandering under the Poliu Ancestral Hall, where is the heroic wind of the iron crossbow?

Today, the sea waves invade the mainland, who can solve the problem of shooting the tide?

Three Tours of Lingyan 206

— Yan Qiao

Lingyan is thirty miles southwest of Suzhou. Its height is only five times that of Tiger Hill, and it has the glory of Qianlong, with a brick-paved imperial road that is very flat, so it takes no effort to go up and down. Even those who are not in good health can barely climb it. I have visited Lingyan three times so far. The first time, I was still studying at Caoqiao Middle School. Although they have not been painted, there are several places where you can sit and talk. There is a train that transports stone foundations and stone steps up the mountain. According to the workers, it can only be transported once from dawn to dusk, which shows how much effort it takes. Mr. Fushiren said. There are also people picking up lime, bricks, tiles, and river sand. They are also hired by mountain farmers, who are paid two cents per pound. So the life of mountain farmers is best to carry sedan chairs, but unfortunately there are only spring and autumn seasons, when there are more tourists, there will be customers. I said, the women at the foot of the mountain are really admirable. They farm when they are busy. They embroider when they are idle. They carry sedan chairs when they are busy and idle. They are talented in both civil and military affairs and can do both rough and fine work. May I ask which country's women in the world have this ability? Even Fayun Temple near Baitaqiao is writing "Great Unity Doctrine, only Buddhism. The way to hygiene, vegetarian food is the most suitable." on the yellow walls, which is probably also influenced by him. Buddhism should be so widespread, then Buddhism will be even more boundless.

The stone of Lingyan Mountain is as simple as Tianping. Originally, there was a famous "Turtle Looking at the Great Lake", but now it is carved with the three characters "Looking at the Buddha", which can turn vulgarity into elegance. If people who like to do things propose more names and add more comments, it can also make the famous mountain more beautiful. There are very few trees on the mountain. Although they have been planted recently, they are still young. It is best to plant more plum blossoms, peach blossoms, and the like. The spring color will be even more gorgeous.

A few days ago, Chinese Qingming and Foreign Qingming met happily. The ships were connected, and the beautiful spring was dancing. After sweeping the tombs, they climbed the mountains to visit. No wonder the mountains were unusually lively. The Shijia Hotel was always full of customers, and I sold tens of millions of sesame cakes. So the scenic line and the life line are interconnected.

Special Symptoms and Treatment Methods of Neutrodyne Radios 207

— Ming Xiang

Neutrodyne radios often have a special strange symptom, that is, in a section with a higher frequency, the radio reception is very good, but the sound of receiving radio stations with a lower frequency is very weak, and sometimes it cannot be received at all. This strange phenomenon may be a problem that service radio workers often encounter and think about most. The main cause of this difficulty usually has the following two types:

(1) The capacitance of the padding capacitor does not match the frequency of the intermediate amplifier of the Neutrodyne radio. The frequency is the difference between the oscillation frequency of the oscillation stage and the frequency of the external signal. For example, if the frequency of the intermediate amplifier stage is I75KC, the oscillation circuit must always be I75KC higher than the high frequency amplifier circuit.

For all adjustment circuits, the frequency that can be tuned depends entirely on the product of the inductance and capacitance of the coil, which is simply represented by LC. The basic formula for calculating the frequency is F=2NLC=I. If you examine the formula carefully, you can see that the product of LC is inversely proportional to the square of the frequency. If you double the frequency, LC must be reduced to a quarter of the original value. If you triple the frequency, LC must be reduced to one-ninth of the original value. For example, if the frequency is 500KC (that is, a wavelength of 600 meters), the required LC product is ·I, then the LC of I000KC should be ·025, which is a quarter of the original number. The LC of I500KC should be ·0III, which is one-ninth of the original value. The frequency range of broadcast radios is from I500KC to 500KC. The highest frequency is three times the lowest, so the maximum capacitance of the adjustment capacitor in the high-frequency stage must be nine times the minimum capacitance to be applicable.

The frequency of the oscillation stage should be I75KC higher, and its frequency range should be I675KC to 675KC. The ratio of the highest to the lowest is two and a half times, so the maximum capacitance of the adjustment capacitor needs to be equal to 21/2 squared (that is, 6I/4) times its minimum capacitance. However, the adjustment capacitors of the high-frequency stage and the oscillation stage of ordinary radios are coaxial, so a capacitor must be connected in series in the oscillation stage to reduce the total capacitance, so that the maximum is 6I/4 times the minimum. This capacitor connected in series is called a padding capacitor. The figure shows the simple adjustment circuit of the high-frequency stage and the oscillation stage of the Neutrodyne radio. C is the padding capacitor, and the capacitance is as indicated in the figure. If the reader thinks about it a little, he should be able to understand its calculation method. If the capacitance of this capacitor does not match, then even if it is calibrated to I675KC when the capacitance is the smallest, it will be far from the predetermined I675KC when it is turned to the largest capacitance, so that the radio cannot receive sensitively. Therefore, the first treatment method for this symptom is to calibrate the capacitance of the padding capacitor.

(2) The oscillation tube stops oscillating. Sometimes the oscillation stage of the Neutrodyne radio can oscillate in the section with a higher frequency (shorter wavelength), but when it is rotated to a lower frequency (longer wavelength), the vacuum tube stops oscillating, so that no radio stations can be heard in that section. This situation is also the most common cause of illness. The reason why the vacuum tube cannot oscillate is probably due to (1) the screen voltage is too low, (2) the curtain grid voltage is too low, (3) the vacuum tube is old and has lost its original efficiency, (4) insufficient feedback energy, etc. Treatment methods: First measure the voltage of the screen electrode and the curtain grid electrode. If it is too low, pay attention to whether the resistance in the screen circuit and the curtain grid circuit is damaged or changed in value, and whether the capacitor has leakage or short circuit. Then check whether the vacuum tube is intact. If there is another vacuum tube of the same number in the machine, you may exchange it for a test, and there will often be unexpected gains. Finally, the feedback energy of the screen circuit should be matched. Increasing the capacitance of the feedback capacitor and the coupling density of the feedback loop are extremely effective. In short, this vacuum tube must be able to obtain extremely stable oscillation within the required frequency range.

Design of Power Amplifiers (Continued) 209

— Jian

As shown in the above formula (3), if RO and RP are equal, then the output P should be:

P = 9 X 784 X 2000 / (2000 + 2000)^2 = 0.882 watts. If RO and RP are equal, then the following formula can be obtained:

P(Max) = U^2 EG^2 / 4RP ·····(4)

P(max) is the maximum output. If the values from the previous example are substituted into formula (4), the result will be the same, that is, P(max) is the maximum output. If the numerical values from the previous example are substituted into formula (4), the result will also be the same, that is, P(max) = 9 X 784 / 4 X 2000 = 0.882 watts. However, to ensure that the power tube operates properly without distortion, the external total resistance RO must adopt an appropriately large value. If the value of RO is too low, distortion is likely to occur. Therefore, to obtain the maximum undistorted output from a power tube, the value of the ordinary external total resistance RO should be twice the value of the plate dissipation resistance RP, namely:

RO = 2RP

In this case, the maximum undistorted output is

P(max) = 2u^2 Eg^2 / 9Rd ··(5)

EG in formula (5) is the effective value, but because the value of the input AC voltage (peak voltage) must not exceed the DC bias voltage value, if this point is taken into consideration, and assuming Eg is the peak voltage, then formula (5) can be changed to the following formula:

P(max) = U^2 Eg^2 / 9RP ··(6)

Taking the 245-type vacuum tube as an example, the maximum undistorted output is calculated. According to the tube's parameters, RP = 1900, u = 3.5. Substituting these numbers into formula (6) yields the following maximum undistorted output:

P(max) = 3.5 X 3.5 X EG^2 / 9 X I900

= 0.67 Eg^2 / I000 watts = 0.67 Eg^2 kilowatts

The peak voltage of EG is 50 volts, i.e., P(max) = 0.67 X 0.2 = I.675 kilowatts. Now, the output of various commonly used power tubes is calculated according to the above, and a table is obtained as follows for readers to refer to when designing power amplifiers.

From the results of the calculation, we can know that the output power is proportional to the grid voltage Eg. For example, when using a 245-type tube, if the voltage of Eg is too low, its capability cannot be fully utilized, which is the most important thing in designing a power amplifier.

The second diagram shows the circuit using a 245-type tube for the final stage power amplification. To make the final stage power amplification tube V3 obtain the maximum output, Eg should be supplied with a peak voltage of 50 volts. This voltage is obtained from the secondary coil of the low-frequency transformer T2. Therefore, if T2 has a ratio of one to four, the voltage of the primary coil E3 should be

E3 = 50 / 4 = 12.5 volts

That is, a voltage of 12.5 volts is required in the plate circuit of the V2 vacuum tube, and this voltage is obtained from the following formula, namely E3 = U^2 E2

In the formula, E2 is the input voltage of the V2 vacuum tube, and U2 is the effective amplification factor of the V2 tube. Therefore, the input voltage E2 of the V2 tube should be

E2 = E3 / U = 12.5 / 6 = 2.08 volts

Secondly, the transformer TI has a ratio of one to three, so E3 should obtain E1 = 2.08 / 3 = 0.669 volts

That is, if there is a voltage of 0.669 volts in the plate circuit of the detector tube VI, the maximum power of the 245-type tube can be obtained. (End)

Points to Note When Making Your Own Power Transformer (Continued) 210

— Bingyi

(3) Calculation of Position: When the wire is not yet wound, use a pencil to draw the width of the iron core window on a piece of white paper. Then calculate how much thickness the primary coil needs in total (when calculating, the thickness of the insulating paper and insulating cloth should be added), how much thickness the secondary coil needs, add the paper core and insulating cloth, and the insulating cloth between the primary and secondary coils. How much is the total thickness? See if this gap is suitable to decide on the winding plan, so that there will be no problem of not being able to fit it at the end.

(4) The iron core should not be too thick to avoid heat generation due to eddy currents and loss of electrical energy.

(5) It is not advisable to use thick paper for insulation. When the position is wide, thick paper is used for insulation in the belief that it can be extra safe. However, thick paper easily stores heat, which is greatly contrary to durability. (6) Coil Taps: The more coil taps, the more important the insulation problem is. Each tap should preferably be cleverly arranged at either end of the coil. The soldering wire should be flat, and the soldered area should be varnished after soldering. Flat wires are best for lead wires so they can be equally attached when winding the lower layer. When at the high-voltage section of the coil, the lead wire must be thin, but at both ends of this high-voltage coil and the lead wires soldered to each tap, thicker wires should be used. The taps should not be pulled too tight, as there is often a danger of pulling them out of the coil.

(7) Pay attention to short circuits. Short circuits are often caused by a short circuit in one turn of the coil, which generates a voltage between the short circuits. This causes a large amount of current to pass through, burning out this circuit, rendering the entire thing ineffective.

(8) Add Wax to the Coil: After the coil is wound, soak it in wax. Do not use gelatinous substances such as rosin resin, because when the enameled wire encounters these things, the wrapping paint will easily dissolve, and because they are prone to moisture, the coil will not dry.

(9) Tighten the Iron Core: After the iron sheets are inserted into the coil, they should be tightened with iron clips to prevent the iron sheets from vibrating and causing AC noise. It is best to paint them firmly with asphalt or magnetic paint.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

Rogers' Mission to China 212

— Yafei

Not long ago, after the United States announced Roosevelt's policy of raising the price of silver, it aroused great attention from all levels of society in our country. Some people advocated banning the export of silver in case of emergency, while others advocated levying a silver tax, taking the method of prohibition through taxation. However, these are all stopgap measures!

Recently, in order to thoroughly understand the impact of raising the price of silver and purchasing power in the Far East, Rogers specially sent Professor Rogers and silver expert Mr. Burton to China for an on-the-spot investigation. The group arrived in Shanghai on the morning of the 9th and stated that they needed to inspect Nanjing, Tianjin, and other places. They will stay in China for about a month. However, according to our speculation, Rogers' sending Rogers to China for investigation this time actually bears two major missions; here, our countrymen, must pay attention to it.

(1) Since Rogers promoted the Blue Eagle Movement, the financial structure of the US authorities has become increasingly shaken. The surge of labor unrest cannot be restrained. One wave after another has continued to expand and spread in various places. Six or seven thousand unemployed workers marched in teams, disturbing the government, and shouting "We need bread and work." The brewing of this labor unrest has developed uncontrollably, so Rogers' Blue Eagle Movement has suffered a major blow, and its fundamental plan has also lost its effectiveness. In order to cope with the current difficult environment, he had to raise the price of silver in order to dump their surplus products in the Far Eastern market, on the one hand to relieve the livelihood of unemployed workers, and on the other hand to reverse the decline of domestic industry and commerce. However, in order to facilitate dumping and encourage the purchasing power of our people, Rogers was sent to China to investigate the commercial situation in various parts of our country and the impact of raising the price of silver.

(2) Rogers also wants to implement his unique authoritarianism to adapt to the current international crisis. Therefore, he ordered Rogers to come to the Far East to investigate the situation of various countries and the current situation of the localities, make an accurate perspective, and be prepared, so that his country can be confident and fearless, so as to handle his entire policy; the depth of his intention is admirable!

From this speculation, the reason why Rogers came to China to investigate, not hesitating to travel far, is not difficult to trace according to the map. Because his coming to China is not only to investigate the silver problem, but also has other important tasks. It is said that the banking industry is also afraid of external suspicion, so it did not go to meet Rogers upon his arrival in Shanghai. However, even though it is like this now, it may not prevent people from generating doubts in the future. In short, they should still check and be cautious in fact, then the outside world's misunderstanding will not be worth fearing. According to reports; when reporters from this city asked Rogers for various opinions, the answers were all elusive, which could not help but arouse suspicion. However, we finally unexpectedly heard a beautiful praise; "I think China is a very promising country"! It is really an honor, which makes us feel "It is impolite to refuse it" and "Ashamed to accept it"! Our China is still seen by Rogers as hopeful, even extremely hopeful! It cannot help but make people feel "A child can be taught"!

Law and Human Sentiment - Watching the Fugitive 213

— Yiping

Human society is gradually evolving, and divine teachings can no longer cope with the progress of this society. In order to protect the peace of human beings in society, laws were produced. It governs all human beings in society with supreme and unlimited power, but the law is a dead trap. It makes a wooden shackle and forces living human beings to drill into the empty space of the wooden shackle, so the law can only make positive judgments, but cannot see through the back side that the law cannot pay attention to. For example, let's say that a car ran over a pedestrian, and naturally this car has to be subject to a certain kind of judgment in terms of law. The law must say that the murderer pays for his life (I don't understand the law, and I haven't had a clear relationship with the law. I think that the murderer pays for his life. There must be such a clause in the law.) But the law cannot make a human judgment on the situation at the time of the event. This dead wooden shackle locks up a living chauffeur. It is not necessarily the chauffeur's fault that the chauffeur ran over the pedestrian. In his driving profession, he must also often want to avoid such unfortunate events. He would never intentionally run the car into a pedestrian, however, I did not say that the pedestrians who were run over by cars all went to seek death on their own. In short, within the scope of the law, a small thing is sometimes a contradiction that the law absolutely did not expect. But the law is supreme, it wants to exercise its authority, and there are countless facts that are absolutely contrary to it.

Alan in The Fugitive wanted to seek the grand plan of developing his engineering, but finally became impoverished and destitute, and was forced by hooligans to become a thief. He had no premeditation. In the event at that time, he was in the same position as the shopkeeper. He was forced to be a robber who killed and stole goods once. Whether Alan was willing or whether he joined the gang of thieves because of this is not told to us in the picture. However, the law sentenced him to ten years of hard labor with a dead wooden shackle.

After he escaped from prison, changed his name and surname, and engaged in his beloved engineering career, it can be seen that Alan is not a bad guy who is willing to be a thief. However, the law knows that he is a fugitive thief, and he was sent into the dead wooden shackle again. We can make a human discussion about the former and the latter. He was forced to become a thief, just as the chauffeur who ran over a pedestrian sometimes really had no choice. The law cannot see the back side. Secondly, it seems that the law does not allow a criminal to repent. Once you become a robber, there is never a chance to turn over. Alan's second prison break can only be "I'm leaving" and he will end his life as a fugitive.

As for the exposure of the darkness of American prisons, which are called civilized by the world, in this film, the film review has described it in detail. Almost every picture grabs the soul of the audience. No wonder the authorities in the concession banned it. So I also want to talk about whether a person who has committed a crime should be beaten, insulted, and forced to perform hard labor like cattle and horses?

By the West Lake (Part 2) 214

— Danxin

In that Yue Lao Temple, there are many young men in suits and fashionable girls; these seem to be middle school and college students from Shanghai. One by one, they kowtowed to Yue Lao, shook the lottery tube, and scrambled to draw lots. After drawing a lot, they spent four copper coins to buy a lottery slip from the incense vendor. After reading the lottery slip, they all left happily and joyfully. "Then, isn't smoking harmful to the lungs?"

"But isn't it much better than wandering the streets and starving?"

"Can't I do other things well?"

"I can't get any jobs anyway. There is overproduction in society, and layoffs are not keeping up. Plus, I don't know how many reserve armies of industry have run out of bankrupt rural areas. By the time I have a job to do, society should have been stained with a layer of hot blood." When speaking excitedly, he almost knocked over the ink bottle on the table.

But our Old Li's brain is not like a machine, which will produce a lot of Inspiration when smoking. At that time, he walked out of the small room and paced towards the gathering place of so-called lower-class people, saying that he was looking for materials among the lower classes.

The life of投稿 with breakfast but no dinner lasted for a year, but the physique of a twenty-year-old youth became almost a middle-aged man around thirty years old.

I haven't seen our Old Li for more than a month. Suddenly, this morning, I received a letter from his hometown. He was sick. He had been sick in Shanghai for a week. Because he had no money for medical treatment, he had to lie hard on the bed. But later, he really had no choice but to call a friend to accompany him back to his hometown. He said: My friends, don't move forward in literature anymore. That is a cruel dead end of hunger and ice!

Listening to the sound of spring rain dripping outside the window, looking at Old Li's letter full of blood and tears, I couldn't help but sigh; "Alas, Old Li has failed!"

A Returnee from Japan Talks (1) 215

— Wangwo

In Japan, which is in a state of emergency, the cover of every magazine is marked with "How should we prepare for the state of emergency?" Every head, young and old, is shaking with the seriousness of 1936. How should we prepare!

Tokyo, after the great earthquake, has been rebuilt, brand new. In particular, primary education is especially valued. Just the construction and internal facilities of primary school buildings alone cost millions! The reason is very simple: every child must recognize the greatness of national power!

Let's talk about some of Japan's clothing, food, housing, and transportation.

Ordinary people wear kimonos made of original-width cloth, which do not need to be cut, and are easy to be changed for other uses when they are not suitable. Students all have bald heads and wear light student uniforms. Teachers and other higher-class people all wear suits, which is probably the trend after the Restoration.

Japanese restaurants have Japanese, Chinese, and Western cuisine, but the latter two have been Japanized, only using the cooking methods and forms. In addition to liking cold food, every meal is suitable for nutritional nourishment, and there are also fruits to help digestion. Speaking of their physique, it is really different from the past! Schools attach great importance to physical education, hygiene, and labor, with complete facilities, as well as various trips, mountain climbing, and summer facilities at the beach, all of which are implemented practically. If it doesn't take long, they will call us Chinese dwarfs, right?

May I Be Reborn as a Daughter 216

— Non

Not long ago, after reading Mr. Qun Ping's article "Wishing to Be Reborn as a Son in the Next Life" in this publication, I couldn't help but feel a sense of aversion. Thus, I want to unleash the pent-up emotions that have been brewing within me for years, a large amount of words that I've long wanted to express but haven't been able to.

The thing is, I harbor a contradictory psychology towards all kinds of women; jealousy, admiration; but I don't know if it's more jealousy or more admiration, which even I find inexplicable!

However, I still think being a woman is good. No matter what aspect, they always have more advantages compared to men. In law, in social interactions, in life, they can more easily gain advantages over men. "Those who did not cultivate good karma in their past lives are reborn as men in this life to suffer!" In times of boredom, I often lament myself this way; if I were a woman, a modern, fashionable woman. Then, no matter what, I wouldn't have to suffer as much as I do now. "Thus, the hearts of parents throughout the land favor the birth of daughters over sons!" Bai Letian said so in "The Song of Everlasting Regret," and the present era has confirmed it for him in an undeniable way. So, while they may be slightly inferior in name, they are far superior in material enjoyment and financial provision. If you don't believe me, feel free to listen to what I have to say; if you are willing to go to the market and investigate, then you will easily find the following examples: fragrant, beautiful, sweet-smelling, delicate, graceful, charming, gorgeous, sensual – all the sweet and enchanting adjectives are monopolized by them, leaving us stinky men to only salivate with desire. Just looking at these aspects is enough for you to be jealous and envious. But men are different, full of stench, sweat, foul breath, a stench that fills the air, making people disgusted! I think the literati of the past were truly hateful; why did they describe women as so lovely and despise men as worthless? What was their intention?

Let's talk about enjoyment! Then, there will naturally be many men, with whiskers and eyebrows, who do their best to serve them, willing to be beasts of burden, not daring to disobey the Jade Emperor's decree, "They can shake the heavens and earth, but they dare not offend the Jade Emperor." That's right, absolutely correct. Although some people say that Chinese women were oppressed by men in the past, oppressed for over four thousand years without a chance to turn over. However, I believe that not only was it like this in the past, but how much different is it now? Every day, they dress up in flamboyant attire, willing to offer their entire bodies, smiles, and nakedness for men to play with and appreciate! For them, it is instinctive to enjoy the rewards, materials, and sexual desires that they exchange for their bodies and smiles, spending extravagantly and consuming limitlessly. On the other hand, men suddenly have an increased burden of pressure; of course, the instability and economic downturn of the current society are at least partly their responsibility. The country has been brought to this state, and it is not unrelated to them. In general, female students and modern ladies are willing to marry important figures as concubines – why is this? Two young men, for the sake of loving the same woman, are willing to sacrifice, becoming irreconcilable, even disregarding injury to their lives and ruin to their careers! The Tang Emperor, for the sake of Yang Yuhuan, disregarded his vast empire, "Loving beauty more than the country"! I ask, which is more important, "country" or "beauty"? All these things are nothing but for the sake of a woman, "Alas, how many people are lost in the inch of land in their hearts!" What exactly is a woman worth? To cause such a scramble for her! So, some people say that if there were no women and money in the world, there would truly be days of peace, times of tranquility. Otherwise, it's all just self-inflicted trouble, with no meaning! Women are a source of trouble, alas! I don't want to say more.

Now women have been elevated almost beyond the thirty-third heaven. In the near future, I'm afraid we men's rice bowls will be smashed to pieces by them, alas! Men are in danger!

But I have to say it again. Ultimately, these things are the sons' own fault, perhaps self-inflicted, so of course, we cannot solely blame women. However, it is undeniable that women are happier than men, so I want to "be reborn as a daughter in the next life" and I have my reasons…

Amateur Mailbox

I Can't Justify It to My Own Conscience 217

Dear Editor:

I have a friend, Mr. Jiang, who has a difficult problem to solve, causing him great mental distress. For the sake of friendship, I want to alleviate his suffering, but I myself cannot solve this problem for him. Because I know you are a guide to society, I am specifically asking you to guide him!

The facts are like this: My friend, Mr. Jiang, is currently studying at a certain university. Recently, he became engaged to Miss B. Before he was engaged, he was once loved by Miss A, but Miss A is an illiterate country girl, and she had previously been engaged to another man by the orders of her parents and the words of a matchmaker. This engagement has now been dissolved (it is said that the other party was incompetent and did not fulfill the engagement, and Miss A's parents did not want him, so both parties voluntarily dissolved the engagement). As for Miss B! She is a complete middle school student. This time, my friend became engaged to her due to the introduction of someone and the agreement of both parties, and with the permission of their parents. My friend previously only had affection for Miss A and no love for her; it was simply that the falling flower had intentions, and the flowing water was indifferent, so this time he became engaged to Miss B. Who knew that Miss A would suddenly express to my friend at this time; with an attitude of "I will not marry anyone but you," and if she cannot get her wish, she will only commit suicide to repay my friend. My friend saw her such deep affection and righteousness, and his whole heart was occupied by her; but Miss B's feelings for him are also not bad, and he has already carried out the engagement. Therefore, my friend is in a dilemma. To serve Qi or to serve Chu? He is unable to cope.

If he chooses Miss B and abandons Miss A, then if Miss A commits suicide, my friend will not only be unable to face her, but he will also not be able to justify it to his own conscience. If he chooses Miss A and abandons Miss B, it is also not easy, because now both parties have willingly engaged, and Miss B is an intellectual, moreover, their feelings for each other are also not bad. If he accepts both, then not only will it not be allowed by Miss B (Miss B certainly does not know about Miss A, but Miss A knows about the engagement with Miss B), but it will also not be tolerated by society. So, what should he do? Please advise in your publication in the near future! With best wishes for your writing, Zhang Xiaochang

Answer: Your friend's kind of problem cannot be solved by outsiders. Because an outsider's answer only stands on the position of reason, while matters such as "love" and "marriage" are mostly manipulated by the feelings of those involved. Therefore, the method that others come up with, even if it is said eloquently, will still seem to the person who wants to apply it to reality that the method drafted by others is unrealistic and cannot appreciate their suffering. What's more, this is a problem of a love triangle, which is most likely to make people fall into depression, and the deadlock with no solution naturally makes the words of others even more useless. However, since you have sincerely inquired, the editor is also very willing to discuss this issue, just for your friend's reference.

The reason why love triangles are difficult to solve is that the one being loved loves both of the two parties who love him, wanting both, but one cannot have both, so "choice" becomes a big problem. If both parties have the determination of "no one but him," there is even less way. "Choosing" is also very simple to say: marrying A means not marrying B, marrying B means not marrying A, extremely simple, what's so difficult? However, it is difficult to make a choice that "is worthy of others and unworthy of oneself." But this is not really impossible, but three principles should be paid attention to: (1) Take his own (for example, your friend) future happiness or career development as the premise, that is, compare the two people to see which one is suitable for him as a spouse; (2) Compare the situation of the two parties. If it is more difficult for one party to marry someone else, then even if your love for her is worse, you cannot be too selfish; (3) Consider the responsibility that you should bear to the other party, such as if you do not marry her, it has the nature of deception. If the above three conditions conflict with each other, then the third and second should be used as the standard. In conclusion, love and marriage should of course be based on one's own opinion, but if one has previously expressed to someone or accepted "love," then one has to take responsibility and cannot completely start from self-interest, let alone change one's mind easily and talk about love with others at will.

Your friend's situation, according to the above conditions, should have two judgments: that is, if your friend has never really expressed love to Miss A before, then even if Miss A threatens to die, he can ignore it; because according to the theory of love, your friend does not need to bear any responsibility, so there is no place to be sorry for her, and her suicide is either too infatuated or too arrogant. However, according to the editor's guess, even if your friend did not have the heart to love Miss A before, I am afraid that he only had a little expression of love in form (at least Miss A meant this), so now if he wants to abandon her, he cannot help but feel a little guilty! Moreover, in fact, A is a country girl, and B is a "complete middle school student," then it is easier to choose the latter for marriage. Therefore, according to the editor's opinion, even though your friend has an engagement with Miss B, he should still not fulfill the engagement and marry Miss A. Of course, this is sorry for B, but between two evils, take the lesser one. It is undoubtedly less harmful to take A and abandon B than to take B and abandon A. Editor

Between Flesh and Blood (2) 219

— Manzhi

Pu Ning answered, "Yes, the eldest young master has returned."

"Returned! Returned!" Sixth Master said as if he was going crazy, clenching his fists and walking back and forth in the study. Pu Ning was still standing there, not daring to move. His eyes followed Sixth Master's body as he turned around in the room. Sixth Master suddenly stopped in front of the window, his eyes looking at the green banana trees outside, beaten by the rain. He stood for a while and then turned back to walk. After walking for a while, he stopped in front of the desk under the window, suddenly hitting the desk with his fist and shouting loudly,

"Kill himself!"

Master said again,

"Beat him to death!"

Saying this, he turned back to walk. Pu Ning thought in his heart, "Sixth Master is mad with anger! The eldest young master is really an unfilial son. If he hadn't followed others in making trouble back then, Sixth Master wouldn't dislike him so much! People with fields and land at home also followed others in making trouble, really deserve to be beaten."

Sixth Master walked to the center of the room, suddenly stopped again, and said to Pu Ning,

"Don't leak the news, understand?"

Pu Ning replied, "I know, Sixth Master."

Sixth Master instructed him again, "Tell Madam and Young Mistress not to let him leave today. I'll come over from Second Master's side."

Pu Ning answered, "Yes," and went out. Sixth Master took a paper umbrella and went out. Second Master's study was not far away. Sixth Master hurried through the rain, turning corners and arriving. At the door, he heard Sixth Master's eldest young master, Lian Sun, loudly saying, "As long as there's money to be made, who cares whether it's Japan or not? Patriotic enthusiasm is all deceiving people!" He also heard the eldest young master of the Third House, Gui Sun, loudly saying, "They are really cold-blooded animals! The Northeast provinces can be lost, and the entire China can be lost. They only care about making money and don't care about the fall of the country. What's the benefit of being a slave to a fallen country?" He also heard Lian Sun say, "Cold-blooded animal or slave to a fallen country, I don't care what people scold me!" Sixth Master covered the paper umbrella and walked through the corridor to the door of the study, coughed, and then went in. Lian Sun and Gui Sun stopped arguing and stood up from their chairs to greet him, calling out,

"Sixth Uncle, please sit down!"

Lian Sun was already over thirty years old, with a round face and a big mouth, looking very much like his grandfather, but he hadn't grown a beard yet. Gui Sun was also around thirty, but he looked like a monkey. Sixth Master usually praised these two nephews highly. Both are capable, one runs a cloth shop in Shantou, and the other runs a sugar warehouse in the city. After Sixth Master sat down, he first asked his nephew Lian Sun, "When did you return home from Shantou?" Lian Sun replied, "Today." He also asked his nephew Gui Sun, "Have you imported any sugar these days?" Gui Sun replied, "We can't import any more. The sugar companies in Shantou bought Japanese sugar in Hong Kong, converted it into sugar water, put it in iron boxes and falsely reported it as Hong Kong sugar water imports, and then sold it after processing. It's especially cheap, and all kinds of sugar have been hit hard, falling by several yuan. It looks like it will fall even more." Sixth Master understood the reason for their argument just now. Unwilling to listen to their argument any longer, he didn't ask any further questions and turned to ask Lian Sun, "Where did your father go?" Lian Sun replied, "He went to the back. He'll be here soon. Sixth Uncle is smoking opium in the cigarette shop."
